## Idea

An **equivalence** is a map that has a [section](foundation-core.sections.md)
and a (separate) [retraction](foundation-core.retractions.md). This condition is
also called being **biinvertible**.

The condition of biinvertibility may look odd: Why not say that an equivalence
is a map that has a [2-sided inverse](foundation-core.invertible-maps.md)? The
reason is that the condition of invertibility is
[structure](foundation.structure.md), whereas the condition of being
biinvertible is a [property](foundation-core.propositions.md). To quickly see
this: if `f` is an equivalence, then it has up to
[homotopy](foundation-core.homotopies.md) only one section, and it has up to
homotopy only one retraction.

## Definition

### The predicate of being an equivalence

### Equivalences

### Components of an equivalence

<pre class="Agda"><a id="2806" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="2813" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2813" class="Module">_</a>

## Properties

### A map is invertible if and only if it is an equivalence

**Proof:** It is clear that if a map is
[invertible](foundation-core.invertible-maps.md), then it is also biinvertible,
and hence an equivalence.

For the converse, suppose that `f : A → B` is an equivalence with section
`g : B → A` equipped with `G : f ∘ g ~ id`, and retraction `h : B → A` equipped
with `H : h ∘ f ~ id`. We claim that the map `g : B → A` is also a retraction.
To see this, we concatenate the following homotopies

```text
         H⁻¹ ·r g ·r f                  h ·l G ·r f           H
  g ∘ h ---------------> h ∘ f ∘ g ∘ f -------------> h ∘ f -----> id.
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="4886" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="4893" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4893" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="4897" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4898" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4898" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="4902" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4902" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="4906" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4908" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4913" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4915" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4916" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4916" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="4919" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4921" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="4925" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4898" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a><a id="4928" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4930" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4931" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4931" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="4934" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4936" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="4940" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4902" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="4943" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4945" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4946" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4946" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="4949" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4951" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4916" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="4954" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4956" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4931" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a><a id="4958" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="4962" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="4971" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4971" class="Function">is-equiv-is-invertible&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="4996" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4998" href="foundation-core.invertible-maps%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1565" class="Function">is-invertibleᵉ</a> <a id="5013" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4946" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="5016" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5018" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1553" class="Function">is-equivᵉ</a> <a id="5028" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4946" class="Bound">fᵉ</a>
  <a id="5033" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4971" class="Function">is-equiv-is-invertible&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="5058" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5059" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5059" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="5062" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="5065" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5065" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="5068" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="5071" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5071" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a><a id="5073" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5075" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5077" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="5079" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5059" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="5082" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="5085" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5065" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="5087" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5089" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="5092" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5093" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5059" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="5096" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="5099" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5071" class="Bound">Kᵉ</a><a id="5101" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="5107" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5107" class="Function">is-equiv-is-invertibleᵉ</a> <a id="5131" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="5137" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5138" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5138" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="5141" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5143" The following maps are not simple constructions and should not be computed with.
Therefore, we mark them as `abstract`.

### Structure obtained from being coherently invertible

### The 3-for-2 property of equivalences

The **3-for-2 property** of equivalences asserts that for any
[commuting triangle](foundation-core.commuting-triangles-of-maps.md) of maps

```text
       h
  A ------> B
   \       /
   f\     /g
     \   /
      ∨ ∨
       X,
```

if two of the three maps are equivalences, then so is the third.

We also record special cases of the 3-for-2 property of equivalences, where we
only assume maps `g : B → X` and `h : A → B`. In this special case, we set
`f := g ∘ h` and the triangle commutes by `refl-htpy`.

[André Joyal](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/André_Joyal) proposed calling this
property the 3-for-2 property, despite most mathematicians calling it the
_2-out-of-3 property_. The story goes that on the produce market is is common to
advertise a discount as "3-for-2". If you buy two apples, then you get the third
for free. Similarly, if you prove that two maps in a commuting triangle are
equivalences, then you get the third for free.

#### The left map in a commuting triangle is an equivalence if the other two maps are equivalences

<pre class="Agda"><a id="10557" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10564" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10564" class="Module">_</a>

#### If the left and right maps in a commuting triangle are equivalences, then the top map is an equivalence

<pre class="Agda"><a id="12104" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="12111" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12111" class="Module">_</a>

#### Composites of equivalences are equivalences

<pre class="Agda"><a id="13575" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="13582" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13582" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="13586" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13587" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13587" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="13591" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13591" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="13595" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13595" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="13599" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13601" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="13606" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13608" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13609" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13609" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="13612" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13614" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="13618" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13587" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a><a id="13621" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13623" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13624" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13624" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="13627" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13629" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="13633" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13591" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="13636" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13638" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13639" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13639" class="Bound">Xᵉ</a> <a id="13642" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13644" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="13648" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13595" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a><a id="13651" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="13655" class="Keyword">where</a>

#### If a composite and its left factor are equivalences, then so is its right factor

<pre class="Agda"><a id="14766" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14773" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14773" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="14777" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14778" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14778" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="14782" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14782" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="14786" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14786" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="14790" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14792" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="14797" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14799" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14800" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14800" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="14803" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14805" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="14809" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14778" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a><a id="14812" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14814" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14815" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14815" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="14818" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14820" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="14824" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14782" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="14827" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14829" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14830" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14830" class="Bound">Xᵉ</a> <a id="14833" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14835" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="14839" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14786" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a><a id="14842" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="14846" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="14855" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14855" class="Function">is-equiv-right-factorᵉ</a> <a id="14878" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="14884" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14885" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14885" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="14888" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14890" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14815" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="14893" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14895" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14830" class="Bound">Xᵉ</a><a id="14897" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14899" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14900" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14900" class="Bound">hᵉ</a> <a id="14903" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14905" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14800" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="14908" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14910" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14815" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a><a id="14912" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14914" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="14920" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1553" class="Function">is-equivᵉ</a> <a id="14930" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14885" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="14933" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14935" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1553" class="Function">is-equivᵉ</a> <a id="14945" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14946" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14885" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="14949" href="foundation-core.function-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#476" class="Function Operator">∘ᵉ</a> <a id="14952" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14900" class="Bound">hᵉ</a><a id="14954" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14956" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14958" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1553" class="Function">is-equivᵉ</a> <a id="14968" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14900" class="Bound">hᵉ</a>
  <a id="14973" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14855" class="Function">is-equiv-right-factorᵉ</a> <a id="14996" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14996" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="14999" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14999" class="Bound">hᵉ</a> <a id="15002" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15002" class="Bound">is-equiv-gᵉ</a> <a id="15014" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15014" class="Bound">is-equiv-ghᵉ</a> <a id="15027" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="15033" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12942" class="Function">is-equiv-top-map-triangleᵉ</a> <a id="15060" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15061" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14996" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="15064" href="foundation-core.function-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#476" class="Function Operator">∘ᵉ</a> <a id="15067" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14999" class="Bound">hᵉ</a><a id="15069" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15071" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14996" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="15074" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14999" class="Bound">hᵉ</a> <a id="15077" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3017" class="Function">refl-htpyᵉ</a> <a id="15088" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15002" class="Bound">is-equiv-gᵉ</a> <a id="15100" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15014" class="Bound">is-equiv-ghᵉ</a>
</pre>
### Equivalences are closed under homotopies

We show that if `f ~ g`, then `f` is an equivalence if and only if `g` is an
equivalence. Furthermore, we show that if `f` and `g` are homotopic equivaleces,
then their inverses are also homotopic.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="15371" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="15378" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15378" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="15382" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15383" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15383" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="15387" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15387" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="15391" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15393" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="15398" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15400" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15401" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15401" class="Bound">Aᵉ</a> <a id="15404" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15406" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="15410" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15383" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a><a id="15413" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15415" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15416" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15416" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a> <a id="15419" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15421" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="15425" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#15387" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="15428" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="15432" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="16051" class="Keyword">abstract</a>

    <a id="17291" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1553" class="Function">is-equivᵉ</a> <a id="17301" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17256" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="17304" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17306" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17256" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="17309" href="foundation-core.function-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#476" class="Function Operator">∘ᵉ</a> <a id="17312" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17271" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="17315" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2800" class="Function Operator">~ᵉ</a> <a id="17318" href="foundation-core.function-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#309" class="Function">idᵉ</a> <a id="17322" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17324" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1553" class="Function">is-equivᵉ</a> <a id="17334" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17271" class="Bound">gᵉ</a>
  <a id="17339" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17180" class="Function">is-equiv-is-sectionᵉ</a> <a id="17360" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17361" class="Argument">Bᵉ</a> <a id="17364" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17366" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17366" class="Bound">Bᵉ</a><a id="17368" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17370" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17371" class="Argument">fᵉ</a> <a id="17374" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17376" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17376" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="17378" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17380" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17381" class="Argument">gᵉ</a> <a id="17384" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17386" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17386" class="Bound">gᵉ</a><a id="17388" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17390" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17390" class="Bound">is-equiv-fᵉ</a> <a id="17402" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17402" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a> <a id="17405" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="17411" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12942" class="Function">is-equiv-top-map-triangleᵉ</a> <a id="17438" href="foundation-core.function-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#309" class="Function">idᵉ</a> <a id="17442" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17376" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="17445" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17386" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="17448" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17449" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3214" class="Function">inv-htpyᵉ</a> <a id="17459" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17402" class="Bound">Hᵉ</a><a id="17461" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17463" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17390" class="Bound">is-equiv-fᵉ</a> <a id="17475" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3949" class="Function">is-equiv-idᵉ</a>

### Any retraction of an equivalence is homotopic to its inverse

    <a id="20184" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20186" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2939" class="Function">is-equiv-map-equivᵉ</a> <a id="20206" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19946" class="Bound">iᵉ</a><a id="20208" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
We will assume a commuting square

```text
        h
    A -----> C
    |        |
  f |        | g
    ∨        ∨
    B -----> D
        i
```

## Equivalence reasoning

Equivalences can be constructed by equational reasoning in the following way:

```text
equivalence-reasoning
  X ≃ Y by equiv-1
    ≃ Z by equiv-2
    ≃ V by equiv-3
```

The equivalence constructed in this way is `equiv-1 ∘e (equiv-2 ∘e equiv-3)`,
i.e., the equivivalence is associated fully to the right.

**Note.** In situations where it is important to have precise control over an
equivalence or its inverse, it is often better to avoid making use of
equivalence reasoning. For example, since many of the entries proving that a map
is an equivalence are marked as `abstract` in agda-unimath, the inverse of an
equivalence often does not compute to any map that one might expect the inverse
to be. If inverses of equivalences are used in equivalence reasoning, this
results in a composed equivalence that also does not compute to any expected
underlying map.

Even if a proof by equivalence reasoning is clear to the human reader,
constructing equivalences by hand by constructing maps back and forth and two
homotopies witnessing that they are mutual inverses is often the most
straigtforward solution that gives the best expected computational behavior of
the constructed equivalence. In particular, if the underlying map or its inverse
are noteworthy maps, it is good practice to define them directly rather than as
underlying maps of equivalences constructed by equivalence reasoning.
